    };
    var tAS = function(EDS) {
        var bSS = ['text', 'search', 'url', 'email', 'tel', 'number'];
        EDS = EDS["toLowerCase"]();
        if (bSS["indexOf"](EDS) !== -1)
            return 0;
        else if (EDS === 'password')
            return 1;
        else

    function AR(a, b, c) {

    var kx = function dC(nC, MC) {
